Holy-Bible---English---Aionian-Bible		1	EAB	Aionian Bible	Aionian Bible	English	English	UK, USA, Canada, Australia, New Zealand				eng	en	en		Creative Commons Attribution 4.0 International, 2018-2026	Creative Commons Attribution 4.0 International	<a href='/Read' title='The Holy Bible Aionian Edition'>AionianBible.org</a> is not one Bible, but a library of public domain and Creative Common Bible texts. In each Bible republication the original text is wholly unaltered, except for this particular translation which is named the <i>Aionian Bible</i> translation. The <i>Aionian Bible</i> translation is a new translation identical to the <a href='/Bibles/English---World-English-Bible-Updated' title='World English Bible Updated'><span class='notranslate'>World English Bible Updated</span></a> except for the retranslation of the <a href='/Bibles/English---Aionian-Bible/Noted' title='262 Aionian Glossary Verses'>two hundred sixty-two verses</a> containing <a href='/Glossary/English---Aionian-Bible' title='Aionian Glossary'><span class='notranslate'>Aionian</span> Glossary</a> words and a few additional verses are revised to correspond with the Hebrew and Greek. This new translation includes the same notes as every Bible in the Aionian Bible library, but also retranslates the <a href='/Glossary/English---Aionian-Bible' title='Aionian Glossary'><span class='notranslate'>Aionian</span> Glossary</a> words to more accurately reflect the underlying Hebrew and Greek words. Every verse retranslation in the <i>Aionian Bible</i> is based on meticulous reference to the underlying Greek and Hebrew text. Learn more about the underlying languages from <a href='/Aionios-and-Aidios' title='Aionios and Aidios explained by Dr. Heleen Keizer and Ramelli and Konstan'>Dr. Heleen Keizer and Ramelli and Konstan</a>. The <a href='/Bibles/English---World-English-Bible-Updated' title='World English Bible Updated'><span class='notranslate'>World English Bible Updated</span></a> was chosen as a base text simply because it is the most readable public domain English translation. Holy-Bible---English---STEPBible-Amalgamant			ESA	STEPBible, Amalgamant	STEPBible, Amalgamant	English	English	UK, USA, Canada, Australia, New Zealand				eng	en	en		Creative Commons Attribution 4.0 International, 2018-2026	Creative Commons Attribution 4.0	Old Testament words are tagged as L = Leningrad (default); Q = Qere 'spoken' corrections from margin and text pointing; K = Ketiv 'written', Tyndale pointing; R = restored text based on Leningrad parallels; and X = extra words from the Septuagint (LXX), in Hebrew, based on BHS and BHK. Other letters indicate parallels and variants with A = Aleppo; B = Biblia Hebraica Stuttgartensia; C = Cairensis; D = Dead Sea and Judean Desert manuscripts; E = emendation from ancient sources, F = format pointing or word division differences without changing letters; H = Ben Chaim (2nd Rabbinic Bible); P = alternate punctuation; S = scribal traditions; and V = variants from other Hebrew manuscripts. Tags place identical sources outside of parens in uppercase. Variant tags are inside parens: uppercase are meaning variants, lower case are minor variants, and differing variants are joined with a “+”. Translators normally follow L, and when this presents a choice between Q and K they follow Q, so K is presented as a variant. Tags in STEP Hebrew are only available when <a href='/Bibles/Hebrew---Hebrew-STEPBible/Genesis/1/parallel-English---STEPBible-Amalgamant'>viewed in parallel with STEP English</a>.<br><br>New Testament words are tagged as N = Nestlé-Aland NA27 edition with NA28 spelling used by most modern translators; K = Textus Receptus (Scrivener 1894) corrected towards the KJV; and O = Greek in other editions not typically used by modern translations or the KJV. NKO without parens (default) means all editions are the same, though the spelling may vary. Lowercase without parens is a minor non-translated word. Variant tags are inside parens: uppercase are meaning variants and lower case are minor variants. Earlier manuscripts were found in North Africa. The NA text relies mostly on these earlier manuscripts, while the TR was compiled from traditional manuscripts. Later scribes occasionally added phrases to clarify the text. Earlier scribes also included words not found in the later manuscripts. So, we have two sets of additions from the earlier and later scribes, apparently to clarify the text with no theological change resulting. For the earliest text, use only words that are in both NA and TR. For clarifications by North Africans as in modern Bibles, include words found only in NA. For clarifications by Byzantines as in the KJV, include words found only in TR, and the TR variants. Holy-Bible---Greek---Greek-STEPBible			GSP	H Καινή Διαθήκη	Greek NT STEP Bible	Ελληνική	Greek, Koine	Greece, Ancient Mediterranean				grc	el	grc		Creative Commons Attribution 4.0 International, 2018-2026	Creative Commons Attribution 4.0	New Testament words are tagged as N = Nestlé-Aland NA27 edition with NA28 spelling used by most modern translators; K = Textus Receptus (Scrivener 1894) corrected towards the KJV; and O = Greek in other editions not typically used by modern translations or the KJV. NKO without parens (default) means all editions are the same, though the spelling may vary. Lowercase without parens is a minor non-translated word. Variant tags are inside parens: uppercase are meaning variants and lower case are minor variants. Earlier manuscripts were found in North Africa. The NA text relies mostly on these earlier manuscripts, while the TR was compiled from traditional manuscripts. Later scribes occasionally added phrases to clarify the text. Earlier scribes also included words not found in the later manuscripts. So, we have two sets of additions from the earlier and later scribes, apparently to clarify the text with no theological change resulting. For the earliest text, use only words that are in both NA and TR. For clarifications by North Africans as in modern Bibles, include words found only in NA. For clarifications by Byzantines as in the KJV, include words found only in TR, and the TR variants. Holy-Bible---Hebrew---Hebrew-STEPBible	RTL		HSB	כתבי הקודש	Hebrew STEP Old Testament	עברית	Hebrew	Israel	rtl	font-ezra.css	font-ezra	hbo	he	he		Creative Commons Attribution 4.0 International, 2018-2026	Creative Commons Attribution 4.0	Old Testament words are tagged as L = Leningrad (default); Q = Qere 'spoken' corrections from margin and text pointing; K = Ketiv 'written', Tyndale pointing; R = restored text based on Leningrad parallels; and X = extra words from the Septuagint (LXX), in Hebrew, based on BHS and BHK. Other letters indicate parallels and variants with A = Aleppo; B = Biblia Hebraica Stuttgartensia; C = Cairensis; D = Dead Sea and Judean Desert manuscripts; E = emendation from ancient sources, F = format pointing or word division differences without changing letters; H = Ben Chaim (2nd Rabbinic Bible); P = alternate punctuation; S = scribal traditions; and V = variants from other Hebrew manuscripts. Tags place identical sources outside of parens in uppercase. Variant tags are inside parens: uppercase are meaning variants, lower case are minor variants, and differing variants are joined with a “+”. Translators normally follow L, and when this presents a choice between Q and K they follow Q, so K is presented as a variant. Tags in STEP Hebrew are only available when <a href='/Bibles/Hebrew---Hebrew-STEPBible/Genesis/1/parallel-English---STEPBible-Amalgamant'>viewed in parallel with STEP English</a>.
